<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>The ownership percentages set forth in this Item 5 include both (i) ownership percentages including the Common Stock issuable upon conversion of the Series D Stock (which Series D Stock, subject to certain exceptions, is non-voting) in the outstanding number of shares of Common Stock (referred to herein as the &#8220;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Deemed Outstanding</font>&#8221;) and (ii) ownership percentages calculated excluding the Common Stock issuable upon conversion of the Series D Stock from the total outstanding number of shares of Common Stock (referred to herein as the &#8220;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Actually Outstanding</font>&#8221;).</font></div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">As of the date hereof, the Reporting Persons collectively may be deemed to beneficially own 36,332,270 shares, which constitute 50.8% of the Deemed Outstanding Common Stock and 62.8% of the Actually Outstanding Common Stock.</font></div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">As a result of the matters described in Item 6 below, Silver Point is no longer a member of a &#8220;group,&#8221; within the meaning of Section 13(d)(3) of the Act and Rule 13d-5(b) thereunder, with THL and Goldman Sachs.&#160;&#160;Therefore, Equity Fund, Advisors and Advisors VI shall no longer be deemed to have an indirect beneficial ownership in the 749,118 shares held by Silver Point.</font></div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">By virtue of the relationships among the Reporting Persons described herein, the Reporting Persons may be deemed to share beneficial ownership with respect to the shares reported herein.&#160;&#160;Except to the extent of a pecuniary interest therein, each of the Reporting Persons expressly disclaims the existence of such beneficial ownership, except: (1) Advisors does not disclaim beneficial ownership of shares held by the THL Coinvest Entities, (2) Advisors VI does not disclaim beneficial ownership of shares held by Equity Fund, Parallel Fund, DT Fund and Fund VI (MG), (3) Putnam Holdings does not disclaim beneficial ownership of shares held by Putnam, and (4) Great-West does not disclaim beneficial ownership of shares held by Putnam and Putnam Holdings.</font></div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">As a result of the matters described in Item 4 above, the Reporting Persons may be deemed to constitute a &#8220;group,&#8221; within the meaning of Section 13(d)(3) of the Exchange Act with Goldman Sachs.&#160;&#160;The Reporting Persons disclaim beneficial ownership of the stock held by Goldman Sachs.&#160;&#160;Neither the filing of this Schedule 13D nor any of its contents shall be deemed to constitute an admission that the Reporting Persons or any of their respective affiliates are the beneficial owners of any of stock beneficially owned by Goldman Sachs for purposes of Section 13(d) of the Exchange Act or for any other purpose.&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Item 6.&#160;&#160;Contracts, Arrangements, Understandings or Relationships With Respect to Securities of the Issuer.</font></div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">&#160;</font><br>
&#160;</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Item 6 is hereby amended by inserting the following as the last paragraph thereof:</font><br>
&#160;</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">&#160;&#8220;As previously disclosed, on March 7, 2011, Silver Point and THL amended the 2009 Letter Agreement to provide that as of the nine month anniversary of the Closing Date, Sections 2 and 3 of the 2009 Letter Agreement would terminate, thus terminating (i) the Proxy and (ii) the Co-Exit Rights.&#160;&#160;In addition, on May 18, 2011, Silver Point, THL and Goldman Sachs amended the Shareholders Agreement to, among other things, provide that Silver Point shall cease to be a party to the Shareholders Agreement as of the nine month anniversary of the Closing Date.&#160;&#160;The Closing Date occurred on May 18, 2011.&#160;&#160;As a result, on February 18, 2012, Silver Point ceased to have any agreement, arrangement or understanding to act together with any other person for the purpose of acquiring, holding, voting or disposing of securities of the Issuer and thus Silver Point ceased to be a member of a &#8220;group,&#8221; within the meaning of Section 13(d)(3) of the Act and Rule 13d-5(b) thereunder, with THL and Goldman Sachs. Therefore, Equity Fund, Advisors and Advisors VI shall no longer be deemed to have an indirect beneficial ownership in the 749,118 shares held by Silver Point.&#8221;</font></div>

<br>
